function scriptLoadCallback(next) {

function loadScript(src, next) {
  if (!src) {
    next();
    return;
  }

  try {
    var scriptTag;

    if (window.hzAsync.firstScript && "async" in window.hzAsync.firstScript) {
      scriptTag = document.createElement("script");
      scriptTag.async = false;
      scriptTag.src = src;
      scriptTag.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
      document.head.appendChild(scriptTag);
    } else if (window.hzAsync.firstScript && window.hzAsync.firstScript.readyState) {
      scriptTag = document.createElement("script");
      window.hzAsync.pendingScripts.push(scriptTag);

      if (scriptTag.addEventListener) {
        scriptTag.addEventListener("load", scriptLoadCallback, false);
      } else if (scriptTag.readyState) {
        scriptTag.onreadystatechange = scriptLoadCallback;
      }

      scriptTag.src = src;
    } else {
      scriptCreationFallback(src);
    }
  } catch (ex) {
    scriptCreationFallback(src);
  }
}

function getCookie(cookieName) {
  var name = cookieName + "=";
  var cookieArray = document.cookie.split(";");
  var i = 0;
  var len = cookieArray.length;

  for (; i < len; i++) {
    var cookie = cookieArray[i];

    while (cookie.charAt(0) === " ") {
      cookie = cookie.substring(1);
    }

    if (cookie.indexOf(name) === 0) {
      return cookie.substring(name.length);
    }
  }

  return "";
}

    img.style.position = "absolute";
    img.style.left = "-100px";
    img.style.width = "1px";
    img.style.height = "1px";
    img.style.top = "-100px";
  } catch (err) {}
}

function getPageTransitionInfo() {
  var trackingValue = getCookie("hzd");
  var metaData = {};

  if (trackingValue && typeof trackingValue === "string") {
    try {
      trackingValue = decodeURIComponent(trackingValue);
      var metaDataList = trackingValue.split(":");

      if (metaDataList.length === 6) {
        metaData.requestId = metaDataList[0];
        metaData.objId = metaDataList[1];
        metaData.compId = metaDataList[2];
        metaData.scopeId = metaDataList[3];
        metaData.posId = metaDataList[4];
        metaData.anchorText = metaDataList[5];
      }
    } catch (ex) {
      metaData = {};
    }
  }

  return metaData;
}

function logPageImpression() {
  if (document.images && HZ.ctx) {
    var eventData = getPageTransitionInfo() || "";
    var requestId = HZ.ctx.rid;

    if (_typeof(eventData) === "object") {
      if (eventData.requestIdOverride) {
        requestId = eventData.requestIdOverride;
        delete eventData.requestIdOverride;
      }

      try {
        eventData = JSON.stringify(eventData);
      } catch (ex) {
        eventData = "";
      }
    }

    var locale = "";
    var siteId = "";

    if (HZ.ctx.geo) {
      locale = HZ.ctx.geo.locale;
      siteId = HZ.ctx.geo.siteId;
    }

    var domainId = -1;

    if (HZ.ctx.domainId) {
      domainId = HZ.ctx.domainId;
    }

    var src = HZ.ctx.logcmd + "evtName=page_impression/" + "evtRequestId=" + encodeURIComponent(requestId) + "/" + "evtMessage=" + encodeURIComponent(eventData) + "/" + "evtLocale=" + encodeURIComponent(locale) + "/" + "evtSiteId=" + encodeURIComponent(siteId) + "/" + "evtDomainId=" + encodeURIComponent(domainId) + "/" + "evtDM=2/" + "evtV=" + encodeURIComponent(HZ.ctx.consentedVisitorIdToken) + "/" + "iid=" + Math.ceil(Math.random() * 1e16) + "/" + "ec=0";
    logEventPixel(src, "page_impression");
  }
}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function (event) {
  if (HZ.ctx.xdEventUrl) {
    loadScript(HZ.ctx.xdEventUrl);
  }

  if (HZ.ctx.eelopi && !HZ.ctx.shouldDeferPageImpressionLogging) {
    logPageImpression();
  }
});

if (HZ && HZ.ctx && HZ.ctx.shouldDeferPageImpressionLogging) {
  var oldOnLoad = window.onload;

  window.onload = function () {
    if (oldOnLoad) {
      oldOnLoad();
    }

    if (HZ.ctx.eelopi) {
      logPageImpression();
    }
  };
}

function supportsES6() {
  try {
    new Function("(a = 0) => a");
    return true;
  } catch (err) {
    return false;
  }
}

window.hzAsync = {
  pendingScripts: [],
  firstScript: document.scripts && document.scripts.length ? document.scripts[0] : null
};

function loadAllScriptsAsync(scriptUrls, callback) {
  var scriptUrl;

  if (scriptUrls) {
    if (!window.Intl && HZ.jbc && HZ.jbc.intlPolyfill) {
      for (var i = 0, len = scriptUrls.length; i < len; i++) {
        if (scriptUrls[i].indexOf("vendor") !== -1) {
          scriptUrls.splice(i + 1, 0, HZ.jbc.intlPolyfill);
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    if (HZ.jbc && HZ.jbc.es6Polyfill && !supportsES6()) {
      for (var j = 0, len1 = scriptUrls.length; j < len1; j++) {
        if (scriptUrls[j].indexOf("vendor") !== -1) {
          scriptUrls.splice(j + 1, 0, HZ.jbc.es6Polyfill);
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    while (scriptUrl = scriptUrls.shift()) {
      if (scriptUrl) {
        loadScript(scriptUrl, function () {});
      }
    }
  }
}
